#### Let's first set up the table to work with by copy+paste into DG the lines below
```
 CREATE TABLE demographics (
  zip int DEFAULT NULL,
  county_code int DEFAULT NULL,
  unique_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  state varchar DEFAULT NULL,
  age int DEFAULT NULL,
  age_bucket varchar DEFAULT NULL,
  gender varchar DEFAULT NULL,
  voter_status varchar DEFAULT NULL
) ;
```

#### Now let's add the data to the empty table we created above:

### Add a target table
```
CREATE TABLE targets (
  unique_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  state varchar DEFAULT NULL,
  persuasion_target int DEFAULT NULL
)
```

### Questions
1. Write a SQL query that returns the number of individuals in Florida who are persuasion targets who fall into each age category. 

2. Write a SQL query that compares the median age of persuasion targets and non-targets, broken down by voter status.

3. Write a SQL query that returns the most populous ZIP code in each county in California and the total population in each ZIP code-county pair
